<script src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery.min.js?ver=3.7.1" id="jquery-core-js" type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1"></script>
<link rel="https://api.w.org/" href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-json/" /><link rel="alternate" title="JSON" type="application/json" href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-json/wp/v2/posts/187106" /><script type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1">
        function reveal() {
                var reveals = document.querySelectorAll("#imark_newsletter, .not-a-thing");
                let bodyElement = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
                for (var i = 0; i < reveals.length; i++) {
                        var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
                        var elementTop = reveals[i].getBoundingClientRect().top;
                        var elementVisible = reveals[i].offsetHeight - 50;
                        var divID = reveals[i].getAttribute('id');
                        if (elementTop < windowHeight - elementVisible) {
                                if(! reveals[i].classList.contains('animate_triggred') ){
                                        bodyElement.classList.add("promote-active");
                                        reveals[i].classList.add("active-promote");
                                }
                        }
                        if ( elementTop < 200 ) {
                                reveals[i].classList.remove("active-promote");
                                reveals[i].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                                bodyElement.classList.remove("promote-active");
                        }
                }
        }

        var animItem = [];
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
                window.addEventListener("scroll", reveal);
                var cookies_disable = '';
                if( getCookie('promote_disable') == 'wait' && cookies_disable == '' ) {
                        var reveals = document.querySelectorAll(".imark_newsletter");
                        reveals[0].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                }
                // reveal();
        });
        
        window.addEventListener("click", function(){
                let bodyElement = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
                var reveals = document.querySelectorAll("#imark_newsletter, .not-a-thing");
                bodyElement.classList.remove("promote-active");
                for (var i = 0; i < reveals.length; i++) {
                        if( reveals[i].classList.contains('active-promote') ){
                                reveals[i].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                        }
                        if( reveals[i].classList.contains('imark_newsletter') ) { 
                                setCookie( 'promote_disable', 'wait', 1 );
                        }
                }
        });

        function setCookie( cname, cvalue, exdays ) {
                const d = new Date();
                d.setTime( d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                let expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;SameSite=Lax" + (location.protocol === 'https:' ? ';Secure' : '');
        }

        function getCookie(cname) {
                let name = cname + "=";
                let ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for(let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                        let c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                                c = c.substring(1);
                        }
                        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                                return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                        }
                }
                return "";
        }

<p>Today, I wanted to share one of my favorite appetizers! I would love for all of my readers to try these bacon-wrapped water chestnuts. They&#8217;re the perfect appetizer for any gathering, whether it&#8217;s a Thanksgiving feast, Christmas dinner, New Year&#8217;s Eve party, or a family reunion.</p>



<p>We always have a variety of appetizers on the table or counter to snack on while preparing the turkey or other main dish and serving all sides at dinner. It&#8217;s so fun to see what each person chooses. The appetizers tend to disappear rather quickly!</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="473" height="710" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;473&#039;%20height=&#039;710&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20473%20710&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts" class="wp-image-187906 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-P-473x710.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-P-473x710.jpeg 473w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-P-233x350.jpeg 233w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-P-768x1152.jpeg 768w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-P.jpeg 800w" data-sizes="(max-width: 473px) 100vw, 473px" /></figure>
</div>


<p>What I love about this appetizer is that, like any other appetizer, it gathers the family together in the kitchen, chatting and reminiscing as we each devour our own.</p>



<p>Each bite-sized bacon-wrapped water chestnut is smothered in the most savory sauce! The brown sugar caramelizes with the bacon, ketchup, and soy sauce as the appetizer cooks. The flavor is out of this world! I can&#8217;t wait to share the recipe with you. Let&#8217;s get to it!</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-ingredients-bacon-wrapped-water-chestnuts"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Ingredients_Bacon-Wrapped_Water_Chestnuts"></span>Ingredients: Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Whole Water Chestnuts</strong> offer a crisp, crunchy texture and a sweet, mild yet nutty flavor in this delicious appetizer! They&#8217;re a corm, a type of tuberous plant, not an actual nut. They&#8217;re grown underground in wet, marshy fields rather than on a tree. It&#8217;s important to use whole water chestnuts vs. sliced ones because they&#8217;re going to be wrapped in bacon. They add fiber, calcium, potassium, carbohydrates, and vitamin C to this appetizer.</li>



<li><strong>Bacon</strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;is salt-cured pork cut from the pig&#8217;s belly or back. It adds a little smoky flavor to any dish. Center-cut bacon or thick-cut bacon is best! Bacon also adds</span> protein to this appetizer.</li>



<li><strong>Ketchup</strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><strong>&nbsp;</strong>is a tangy and sweet condiment made by mixing&nbsp;</span>tomato paste with sugar, vinegar, water, seasonings, and salt.</li>



<li><strong>Brown Sugar</strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><strong>&nbsp;</strong>is a mixture of granulated white sugar and molasses. It’s added for flavor and to help maintain moisture. Brown sugar caramelizes as it bakes, creating a robust,</span> rich flavor that makes these bacon-wrapped water chestnuts truly incredible!</li>



<li><strong>Soy Sauce:</strong> A savory and salty caramel-colored sauce made from soybeans, salt, wheat, and a fermenting agent such as yeast or koji mold.</li>



<li><strong>Dry Mustard Powder</strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;is made from ground mustard seeds. When combined with the wet ingredients, it releases its oils, which add a delicious,</span> robust kick of flavor to this appetizer!</li>
</ul>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Instructions"></span>Instructions<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_One_Gather_The_Ingredients_%E2%80%93_Preheat_the_Oven_%E2%80%93_Grease_9%C3%9713_Pan"></span>Step One: Gather The Ingredients &#8211; Preheat the Oven &#8211; Grease 9&#215;13 Pan<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Gather all the ingredients you need to make this bacon-wrapped water chestnut appetizer. Preheat your oven to (375°F) = (190°C). Grease a 9″ by 13″ pan or rimmed baking sheet with cooking spray.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts Ingredients" class="wp-image-187455 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Two_Cut_the_Bacon_Into_Thirds"></span>Step Two: Cut the Bacon Into Thirds<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Cut the package(s) of uncooked raw bacon into thirds. This creates the perfect-sized strips of bacon to wrap the water chestnuts.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Cut the Bacon into Thirds" class="wp-image-187456 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-1.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-1.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-1-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-1-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-step-three-wrap-the-chestnuts-and-secure-them-with-toothpicks"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Three_Wrap_the_Chestnuts_and_Secure_Them_with_Toothpicks"></span>Step Three: Wrap the Chestnuts and Secure Them with Toothpicks<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Wrap a piece of raw bacon around one water chestnut and secure it with a toothpick. Place the bacon-wrapped chestnuts in the greased pan. Cover each water chestnut with a piece of bacon until all the chestnuts are wrapped.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Wrap The Bacon Around the Chestnuts" class="wp-image-187457 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-2.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-2.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-2-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-2-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Four_Bake_The_Chestnuts_As_Directed"></span>Step Four: Bake The Chestnuts As Directed<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Bake uncovered for 20 minutes at (375<strong>°F</strong>) = (190<strong>°C</strong>). </p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Bake The Wrapped Chestnuts" class="wp-image-187458 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-3.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-3.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-3-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-3-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Five_Remove_The_Grease_Carefully"></span>Step Five: Remove The Grease Carefully<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Then, drain the fat from the pan. This is the hardest part of the whole recipe. Be careful!</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Remove the Grease Carefully" class="wp-image-187459 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-5.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-5.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-5-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-5-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Six_Combine_the_Sauce_Ingredients"></span>Step Six: Combine the Sauce Ingredients<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>It is time to make a delicious and savory sauce! Place the ketchup, brown sugar, soy sauce, and dry mustard in a small bowl and whisk until smooth.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Mix The Sauce With A Spoon" class="wp-image-187460 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-8.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-8.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-8-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-8-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Seven_Pour_The_Sauce_Over_the_Baked_Chestnuts"></span>Step Seven: Pour The Sauce Over the Baked Chestnuts<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Next, cover the baked bacon-wrapped chestnuts with this sauce mixture.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Pour The Sauce On The Water Chestnuts" class="wp-image-187461 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-6.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-6.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-6-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-6-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-step-eight-bake-the-chestnuts-for-another-20-minutes"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step_Eight_Bake_the_Chestnuts_for_Another_20_minutes"></span>Step Eight: Bake the Chestnuts for Another 20 minutes<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Finally, bake for an additional 20-30 minutes. Allow the pan to cool on a cooling rack for a short time. Enjoy!</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts Appetizer" class="wp-image-187462 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-7.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-7.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-7-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/Bacon-Wrapped-Water-Chestnuts-7-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" /></figure>
</div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Bacon-Wrapped_Water_Chestnuts_Recipe"></span>Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts Recipe<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>

									</li>

									</li>

															<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">teaspoon</span>

			<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
		<div class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-color-header">Instructions</div>
				<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
						<div class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-instruction-group-name">Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts Appetizer</div>
						<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Gather all of your ingredients. Preheat your oven to (375<strong>°F</strong>) = (190<strong>°C</strong>) Grease a 9″ by 13″ inch pan. </p></div>
														</li>
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Cut the package(s) of uncooked raw bacon into thirds. This creates the perfect sized strips of bacon to wrap the water chestnuts.</p></div>
														</li>
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Wrap a piece of raw bacon around one water chestnut and secure it with a toothpick. Place the bacon-wrapped chestnuts in the greased pan. Continue to wrap each water chestnut with a piece of bacon until all the chestnuts are wrapped. Place the pan of bacon-wrapped chestnuts on a middle rack in the oven.</p></div>
														</li>
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Bake uncovered for 20 minutes.</p></div>
														</li>

							</ol>
		</div>
				<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">

														</li>
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Cover the baked chestnuts with this sauce mixture.</p></div>
														</li>
								<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
										<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Bake for an additional 20-30 minutes. Enjoy!</p><div class='mailmunch-forms-in-post-middle' style='display: none !important;'></div></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="What_Can_I_Serve_With_Bacon-Wrapped_Water_Chestnuts"></span>What Can I Serve With Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts are a classic party appetizer, crispy, smoky, slightly sweet, and irresistibly crunchy. Because they’re rich and savory, the best side dishes and pairings either balance that richness or complement the bold flavors. Whether you’re serving them for a holiday gathering, game day, or cocktail party, here are the best foods to serve alongside Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Fresh_Light_Pairings_Balance_the_Richness"></span>Fresh &amp; Light Pairings (Balance the Richness)<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Light, refreshing sides help offset the salty bacon and keep the menu from feeling too heavy.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Crisp green salad</strong> with vinaigrette</li>



<li><strong>Fruit platter</strong> (pineapple, melon, grapes, or strawberries)</li>



<li><strong>Coleslaw</strong> with a tangy dressing</li>



<li><strong>Vegetable tray</strong> with ranch or hummus</li>



<li><strong>Cucumber or tomato salad</strong></li>
</ul>



<p>These options cleanse the palate and pair beautifully with bacon’s smoky flavor.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Other_Appetizers_That_Pair_Well"></span>Other Appetizers That Pair Well<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>If you’re building an appetizer spread, these finger foods complement Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts without overpowering them.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Deviled eggs</li>



<li>Stuffed mushrooms</li>



<li>Cheese ball with crackers</li>



<li>Cocktail sausages or little smokies</li>



<li>Shrimp cocktail</li>



<li>Spinach or artichoke dip</li>
</ul>



<p>Together, they create a well-rounded party table with a mix of textures and flavors.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Dips_Sauces_for_Serving"></span>Dips &amp; Sauces for Serving<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>While Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts are flavorful on their own, offering dips gives guests variety.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Sweet-and-sour sauce</li>



<li>Honey mustard</li>



<li>Teriyaki or soy-based glaze</li>



<li>Barbecue sauce</li>



<li>Chili sauce</li>
</ul>



<p>Serve dips on the side to let guests customize each bite.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Main_Dishes_That_Work_Well"></span>Main Dishes That Work Well<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>If these appetizers are part of a larger meal, pair them with simple mains that won’t compete with their bold flavor.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Baked or grilled chicken</li>



<li>Slow cooker pulled pork</li>



<li>Ham or roast beef</li>



<li>Sliders or mini sandwiches</li>



<li>Fried or baked fish</li>
</ul>



<p>Keeping the principal dish simple allows the appetizer to shine.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-can-these-bacon-wrapped-water-chestnuts-be-made-ahead-of-time"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Can_these_bacon-wrapped_water_chestnuts_be_made_ahead_of_time"></span>Can these bacon-wrapped water chestnuts be made ahead of time?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>These bacon-wrapped water chestnuts are a great appetizer to make ahead of time! I recommend wrapping the water chestnuts in bacon, sealing them with a toothpick, and placing them in the greased pan.</p>



<p>Do not cook or add the sauce at this point! I would then store the pan in the fridge for 2-3 days before cooking. When ready, make the sauce and cook as instructed in the recipe.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-can-i-use-worcestershire-sauce-or-sriracha-in-this-bacon-wrapped-water-chestnut-appetizer"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Can_I_use_Worcestershire_sauce_or_sriracha_in_this_bacon-wrapped_water_chestnut_appetizer"></span>Can I use Worcestershire sauce or sriracha in this bacon-wrapped water chestnut appetizer?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>I love the flavor of the soy sauce combined with the other ingredients in this appetizer&#8217;s sauce. You can swap out the soy sauce for Worcestershire sauce if you&#8217;d like. It&#8217;ll give it a slightly different flavor.</p>



<p>Worcestershire sauce is typically made with anchovies, onion powder, garlic powder, and molasses. It tends to be low-sodium, whereas soy sauce has less sugar.</p>



<p>It might be fun to try making the sauce both ways and see what you and your family prefer. Adding a bit of sriracha may also be fun, but remember, a little goes a long way!</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-can-these-bacon-wrapped-water-chestnuts-be-cooked-in-an-air-fryer"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Can_these_bacon-wrapped_water_chestnuts_be_cooked_in_an_air_fryer"></span>Can these bacon-wrapped water chestnuts be cooked in an air fryer?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>I&#8217;m not sure I can recommend cooking these in an air fryer because of the excess bacon grease. I&#8217;m all about easy clean-up; baking these in the oven is much easier. Plus, you need to remove the excess grease, drizzle the sauce over them, and bake them for a few more minutes.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-can-i-use-something-other-than-water-chestnuts-in-this-recipe"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Can_I_use_something_other_than_water_chestnuts_in_this_recipe"></span>Can I use something other than water chestnuts in this recipe?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>I highly recommend using water chestnuts in this appetizer recipe! There is something delicious about the bacon&#8217;s taste, the water chestnuts&#8217; crisp crunch, and the amazing sauce!</p>



<p>If you decide to swap it out, chunks of pineapple or little smokies may be good alternatives.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-i-love-this-appetizer-recipe-check-out-some-of-my-other-favorites"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="I_love_this_appetizer_recipe_Check_out_some_of_my_other_favorites"></span>I love this appetizer recipe. Check out some of my other favorites!<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/pineapple-cream-cheese-dip/"><strong>5 Ingredient Pineapple Cream Cheese Dip</strong></a></li>



<li><a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/cranberry-jalapeno-cream-cheese/"><strong>Cranberry Jalapeño Cream Cheese Spread</strong></a></li>



<li><a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/stuffed-baked-sausage-mushrooms/"><strong>Stuffed Baked Sausage Mushroom Recipe</strong></a></li>



<li><a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/spinach-artichoke-dip/"><strong>Spinach Artichoke Dip</strong></a></li>
</ul>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-final-word"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Final_Word"></span>Final Word<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>Please let me know if you make these savory bacon-wrapped water chestnuts! The taste of the bacon and water chestnuts combined with the sauce is a mouthful of flavors that will make everyone want to go back for another serving and then another!</p>



<p>Bacon-Wrapped Water Chestnuts are a versatile appetizer that pairs beautifully with fresh sides, classic party foods, and simple main dishes. By balancing rich flavors with light, crisp accompaniments, you’ll create a crowd-pleasing menu perfect for holidays, potlucks, and entertaining year-round. May God bless this World, Linda.</p>

			<div class="post-thumbnail-inner">
				<img width="700" height="525" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;700&#039;%20height=&#039;525&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%20700%20525&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image perfmatters-lazy" alt="The Best Hot Chicken Salad" decoding="async" data-src="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/The-Best-Hot-Chicken-Salad-4.jpeg" data-srcset="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/The-Best-Hot-Chicken-Salad-4.jpeg 700w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/The-Best-Hot-Chicken-Salad-4-350x263.jpeg 350w, https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/The-Best-Hot-Chicken-Salad-4-500x375.jpeg 500w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" />			</div>

			<div class="entry-taxonomies">
			<span class="category-links term-links category-style-normal">
				<a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/category/chicken/" class="category-link-chicken" rel="tag">Chicken</a> | <a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/category/dinner/" class="category-link-dinner" rel="tag">Dinner</a> | <a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/category/holidays/" class="category-link-holidays" rel="tag">Holidays</a> | <a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/category/lunch/" class="category-link-lunch" rel="tag">Lunch</a> | <a href="https://www.foodstoragemoms.com/category/recipes/" class="category-link-recipes" rel="tag">Recipes</a>			</span>
